class=\"row\" style=\"transform: none;\">\n<div id=\"df-content\" class=\"df-content col-md-8\" role=\"main\" style=\"position: relative; overflow: visible; box-sizing: border-box; min-height: 1px;\">\n\n\n<div class=\"theiaStickySidebar\" style=\"padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 1px; position: static;\"><div class=\"\">\n<div id=\"post-28511\" class=\"post-28511 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-breakups category-exes category-relationships df-standard\" itemscope=\"\" itemtype=\"http://schema.org/NewsArticle\" itemprop=\"blogPost\" role=\"article\">\n<div class=\"df-post-title  aligncenter\" onclick=\"void(0)\"><div class=\"boxed-wrap\"><div class=\"df-single-category\"><span class=\"entry-terms category\" itemprop=\"articleSection\"><a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/category/relationships/breakups/\" rel=\"category tag\">BREAKUPS</a>, <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/category/relationships/exes/\" rel=\"category tag\">EXES</a>, <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/category/relationships/\" rel=\"category tag\">RELATIONSHIPS</a></span></div><h2 class=\"entry-title  display-3\" itemprop=\"headline\"><a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/when-you-see-your-ex-how-to-not-let-it-unravel-you/\" title=\"WHEN YOU SEE YOUR EX: HOW TO NOT LET IT UNRAVEL YOU\">WHEN YOU SEE YOUR EX: HOW TO NOT LET IT UNRAVEL YOU</a></h2><div class=\"df-post-on\"><time class=\"entry-published updated\" datetime=\"2017-04-16T10:59:15+00:00\" title=\"Sunday, April 16, 2017, 10:59 am\"><a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/2017/04/16/\"><meta itemprop=\"datePublished\" content=\"April 16, 2017\">April 16, 2017</a></time></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"featured-media  filter_bw\"><a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/when-you-see-your-ex-how-to-not-let-it-unravel-you/\"><img width=\"1300\" height=\"975\" src=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/when-you-see-your-ex-natasha-adamo.jpg\" class=\"attachment-full size-full wp-post-image\" alt=\"Natasha Adamo writes about: When You See Your Ex: How To Not Let It Unravel You\" srcset=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/when-you-see-your-ex-natasha-adamo.jpg 1300w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/when-you-see-your-ex-natasha-adamo-300x225.jpg 300w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/when-you-see-your-ex-natasha-adamo-768x576.jpg 768w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/when-you-see-your-ex-natasha-adamo-1024x768.jpg 1024w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/when-you-see-your-ex-natasha-adamo-570x428.jpg 570w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/when-you-see-your-ex-natasha-adamo-330x248.jpg 330w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1300px) 100vw, 1300px\"></a></div>\n<div class=\"entry-content\" itemprop=\"articleBody\">\n<p>So many&nbsp;cultures celebrate holidays, traditions and festivities around the spring equinox – Easter, Holi, Passover, Norooz (the Persian New Year), Hanami (the blossoming of cherry trees in Japan), etc. –&nbsp;<em>Why?</em> Spring is the season of new beginnings. It’s the time of year when everything is in bloom. Animals awaken, the conditions are ideal and everything just comes to life again. The air&nbsp;no longer has the&nbsp;abrasiveness of winter’s chill and everything seems to be in the kind of&nbsp;order that you’re convinced, is how it was always intended to be. So, you commit to and embrace the new beginning, hoping for <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/how-to-let-him-go-get-over-the-pain-of-losing-your-ex/\" target=\"_blank\">your heart to forget</a> an ex that has somehow disabled&nbsp;the switch from ever <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/how-to-get-over-your-ex-in-10-steps/\" target=\"_blank\">shutting off</a>. And then… it happens:&nbsp;you see him. Not just in your head and heart, but right in front of you.&nbsp;<em>What do you do when you see your ex?&nbsp;</em></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><em>What do you do when&nbsp;you’re suddenly face to face with the one person who, despite how deeply they broke your heart, you still compare everyone else to?&nbsp;</em></p>\n<h4>When you see your ex, you convince yourself&nbsp;that everything&nbsp;you’ve worked so hard to glue back together is now irreparably&nbsp;unglued… <em>but it doesn’t have to be that way.</em></h4>\n<p>Years ago, I dated a man that made me feel like I had never experienced anything before him. He redefined it all and was unlike anyone I had ever been in a relationship with&nbsp;– much older, very successful, an intellectual encyclopedia, well spoken, traveled everywhere, had an infectious sense of humor and a personality that was larger than life. I can still hear his laugh. I made many mistakes in the relationship, but his emotional unavailability and <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/no-empathy-how-to-deal-lack-empathy/\" target=\"_blank\">lack of empathy</a> ultimately proved to be a deal breaker that no matter how hard I tried, my <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/people-pleasing-exposed-5-ways-to-stop-being-a-doormat-now/\" target=\"_blank\">disease to please</a> couldn’t salvage. It was one of the most painful breakups I had ever gone through, but after lots of <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/how-to-stop-stalking-your-ex/\" target=\"_blank\">stalking</a> and tears, I finally found a way to put one emotional foot in front of the other (despite terribly&nbsp;<a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/why-do-i-miss-him-the-one-thing-you-need-to-know/\" target=\"_blank\">missing what was</a>).</p>\n<p>Fast forward to about 9 months later. I had just finished having lunch by myself at Spago&nbsp;in Beverly Hills and was waiting for the check. All of a sudden, I.hear.that.laugh. With every antenna up, I turn around and see him in conversation with 2 beautiful&nbsp;women. Before I can look away, we lock eyes. He immediately excuses himself and walks toward me. I don’t remember much of our exchange because there wasn’t much that we exchanged – we said our hellos as quickly as we said our&nbsp;goodbyes. He seemed a bit uneasy, but I was uncharacteristically calm.</p>\n<p>The one thing that I remember more vividly than anything though, was that for the first time in my life, I was INDIFFERENT.&nbsp;It was the weirdest thing. I went about my day after that and didn’t think about it at all. I didn’t even feel the need to tell any of my girlfriends that I had run into him. I didn’t spend the next month comparing myself to the women he was engaged in conversation with, trying to find them on social media or obsessing over how I looked and what I said. Pigs were officially flying.</p>\n<p>That night, I got a text from him saying how great it was to see me. I didn’t respond, deleted it and never&nbsp;heard from him again. There was absolutely no ill will, just pure<em> indifference.</em></p>\n<p>SO, with it being Easter today and the start of a&nbsp;season that’s known for new beginnings, I wanted to share with you how to emotionally navigate when you see your ex.</p>\n<h3 style=\"text-align: center;\">Here’s what to do when you see your ex (&amp; how to not let it unravel you):</h3>\n<p> <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/when-you-see-your-ex-how-to-not-let-it-unravel-you/#more-28511\" class=\"more-link button outline small\">Continue Reading</a></p>\n</div>\n<div df-standard\" itemscope=\"\" itemtype=\"http://schema.org/NewsArticle\" itemprop=\"blogPost\" role=\"article\">\n<div class=\"df-post-title  aligncenter\" onclick=\"void(0)\"><div class=\"boxed-wrap\"><div class=\"df-single-category\"><span class=\"entry-terms category\" itemprop=\"articleSection\"><a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/category/relationships/breakups/\" rel=\"category tag\">BREAKUPS</a>, <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/category/relationships/decoded/\" rel=\"category tag\">DECODED</a>, <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/why-do-i-miss-him-the-one-thing-you-need-to-know/\" title=\"WHY DO I MISS HIM? THE ONE THING YOU NEED TO KNOW\">WHY DO I MISS HIM? THE ONE THING YOU NEED TO KNOW</a></h2><div class=\"df-post-on\"><time class=\"entry-published updated\" datetime=\"2017-04-09T12:07:08+00:00\" title=\"Sunday, April 9, 2017, 12:07 pm\"><a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/2017/04/09/\"><meta itemprop=\"datePublished\" content=\"April 9, 2017\">April 9, 2017</a></time></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"featured-media  filter_bw\"><a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/why-do-i-miss-him-the-one-thing-you-need-to-know/\"><img width=\"1019\" height=\"1186\" src=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/natasha-adamo-why-do-I-miss-him.jpg\" class=\"attachment-full size-full wp-post-image\" alt=\"Why Do I Miss Him? The One Thing You Need To Know\" srcset=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/natasha-adamo-why-do-I-miss-him.jpg 1019w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/natasha-adamo-why-do-I-miss-him-258x300.jpg 258w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/natasha-adamo-why-do-I-miss-him-768x894.jpg 768w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/natasha-adamo-why-do-I-miss-him-880x1024.jpg 880w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1019px) 100vw, 1019px\"></a></div>\n<div class=\"entry-content\" itemprop=\"articleBody\">\n<p>“Why do I miss him?” is something that I’ve continued to ask myself WAY after relationsh*ts have ended and breakups ensued. I’d even find myself wondering “why do <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/how-to-stop-missing-someone-when-youre-heartbroken/\" target=\"_blank\">I miss him</a> (??!)” when I’d be on a date – sitting across from a totally nice guy in a beautiful restaurant; my mind thousands of miles away.</p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\"><em>Even worse… I’d wonder “why do I miss him?” when I was &nbsp;IN A RELATIONSHIP with someone new. </em></h4>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">Someone who had no idea how unfinished my emotional business truly was.</h4>\n<p>Every song that came on, everything that happened or didn’t happen… every.single.moment catered to <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/how-to-let-him-go-get-over-the-pain-of-losing-your-ex/\" target=\"_blank\">highlighting the absence</a> of <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/how-to-get-over-your-ex-in-10-steps/\" target=\"_blank\">what was</a>.</p>\n<p>So, I acquiesced to an existence&nbsp;of someone at the end of their emotional life – always&nbsp;reverting back to the loss of my soulmate, “the one.”&nbsp;My only shot at Happily Ever After that had come and gone.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><em>What do you do when you can’t breakup with your memory?</em></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><em>Will the&nbsp;<a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/heartbroken-on-valentines-day-3-things-to-keep-in-mind/\" target=\"_blank\">heartbreak</a>, thoughts and&nbsp;<a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/how-to-stop-stalking-your-ex/\" target=\"_blank\">obsessive actions</a>&nbsp;EVER end?</em></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">How do you deal with going through the motions of life while your heart is with someone that never gave you&nbsp;<a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/how-to-get-closure-when-you-have-none/\" target=\"_blank\">closure</a>?</p>\n<h3 style=\"text-align: center;\">If you’re still wondering “why do I miss him?” here’s why + the one thing you need to know:</h3>\n<p> <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/why-do-i-miss-him-the-one-thing-you-need-to-know/#more-28471\" class=\"more-link button outline small\">Continue Reading</a></p>\n</div>\n<div itemtype=\"http://schema.org/NewsArticle\" itemprop=\"blogPost\" role=\"article\">\n<div class=\"df-post-title  aligncenter\" onclick=\"void(0)\"><div class=\"boxed-wrap\"><div class=\"df-single-category\"><span class=\"entry-terms category\" itemprop=\"articleSection\"><a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/category/self-improvement/happiness/\" rel=\"category rel=\"category tag\">RELATIONSHIPS</a>, <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/category/self-improvement/self-esteem/\" rel=\"category tag\">SELF ESTEEM</a>, <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/category/self-improvement/\" rel=\"category tag\">SELF IMPROVEMENT</a></span></div><h2 class=\"entry-title  display-3\" itemprop=\"headline\"><a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/self-sabotage-in-relationships-life-3-ways-to-end-it-now/\" title=\"SELF SABOTAGE IN RELATIONSHIPS &amp; LIFE: 3 WAYS TO END IT NOW\">SELF SABOTAGE IN RELATIONSHIPS &amp; LIFE: 3 WAYS TO END IT NOW</a></h2><div class=\"df-post-on\"><time class=\"entry-published updated\" datetime=\"2017-04-01T11:04:56+00:00\" title=\"Saturday, April 1, 2017, 11:04 am\"><a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/2017/04/01/\"><meta itemprop=\"datePublished\" content=\"April 1, 2017\">April 1, 2017</a></time></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"featured-media  filter_bw\"><a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/self-sabotage-in-relationships-life-3-ways-to-end-it-now/\"><img width=\"1002\" height=\"1300\" src=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/self-sabotage-in-relationships-and-life.jpg\" class=\"attachment-full size-full wp-post-image\" alt=\"Self Sabotage In Relationships &amp; Life: 3 Ways To End It Now\" srcset=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/self-sabotage-in-relationships-and-life.jpg 1002w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/self-sabotage-in-relationships-and-life-231x300.jpg 231w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/self-sabotage-in-relationships-and-life-768x996.jpg 768w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/self-sabotage-in-relationships-and-life-789x1024.jpg 789w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1002px) 100vw, 1002px\"></a></div>\n<div class=\"entry-content\" itemprop=\"articleBody\">\n<p><em>+ (doing a little giveaway! details at the end of this post xx)</em></p>\n<p>Self sabotage is the one thing that will destroy&nbsp;your chances of ever fully experiencing&nbsp;the relationships, luck, <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/how-to-be-fearless-confident-start-living-your-dreams/\" target=\"_blank\">confidence</a>, fulfillment,&nbsp;<a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/how-to-reinvent-yourself-reclaim-happiness-in-5-steps/\" target=\"_blank\">happiness</a>, success&nbsp;and <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/15-life-changing-decisions-to-make-for-2017/\" target=\"_blank\">life</a> that&nbsp;you&nbsp;want more than anything.</p>\n<p>Self love and self sabotage can never coexist. If you self sabotage, it means that you embody the enemy&nbsp;while making it your life’s mission to take down the enemy.</p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">“God said ‘Love Your Enemy,’ and so I obeyed Him and loved myself.” – Khalil Gibran</h4>\n<p>When you self sabotage, you make a subconscious agreement with yourself to get&nbsp;off the road of life and onto that attractive and fancy treadmill.&nbsp;The treadmill comforts you because it not only provides PROOF that you’re going the distance and burning calories, it secures proof of productivity as well.</p>\n<p>And if you’re in a destructive pattern like this, proof will always supersede feeling. The treadmill also guarantees the same terrain, weather and outcome&nbsp;every time.</p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">The problem with running on emotional treadmills is that no matter how hard you run (&amp; try to convince yourself that it’ll be different THIS time), you never actually&nbsp;<em>get&nbsp;</em>anywhere. You always end up back at square one.</h4>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">Self Sabotage? <em>Same.</em></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\">Certainty = Safety and as humans, we will risk our own values, goals, best interests and moral compasses to secure a feeling of the kind of safety that certainty provides. <strong>Even if that certainty is our own misery.</strong></p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">Self sabotage is nothing more than an inability to get out of your own way. It’s that hidden mechanism that pulls the rug out from under your life, proving that happiness is never to be trusted – always chased.</h4>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><em>Self sabotage murders who you could&nbsp;become – the Sasha Fierce badbass that your instinct is hungry to birth. </em></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">No matter what you’ve gone through in life, self sabotage is the only way that your destiny can ever be hijacked.</p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">And because you&nbsp;<em>can’t&nbsp;</em>get out of your own way, you end up getting bulldozed every time – surrounded by a manifested&nbsp;environment that does nothing but affirm the necessity of you having to live&nbsp;on your emotional knees – now and forevermore. The End.</h4>\n<p>I’ve self sabotaged my relationships, opportunities, experiences and life for way longer than I’ve been lucky enough to live without the “bad luck,” that I would always tell myself I suffered from (due to the superficial of course: not being pretty, smart, sexy, cool, interesting enough, etc).</p>\n<h3 style=\"text-align: center;\">Here’s how to know if you self sabotage, <em>why</em> you self sabotage &amp; 3 ways to put an end to it NOW…</h3>\n<p> <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/self-sabotage-in-relationships-life-3-ways-to-end-it-now/#more-28438\" rel=\"category tag\">LIFESTYLE</a>, <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/category/lifestyle/wellness/\" rel=\"category tag\">WELLNESS</a></span></div><h2 class=\"entry-title  display-3\" itemprop=\"headline\"><a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/my-everyday-detox-tea-healthy-digestion-healthy-skin/\" title=\"MY EVERYDAY DETOX TEA: BECAUSE HEALTHY DIGESTION = HEALTHY SKIN\">MY EVERYDAY DETOX TEA: BECAUSE HEALTHY DIGESTION = HEALTHY SKIN</a></h2><div class=\"df-post-on\"><time class=\"entry-published updated\" datetime=\"2017-03-26T08:10:34+00:00\" title=\"Sunday, March 26, 2017, 8:10 am\"><a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/2017/03/26/\"><meta itemprop=\"datePublished\" content=\"March 26, 2017\">March 26, 2017</a></time></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"featured-media  filter_bw\"><a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/my-everyday-detox-tea-healthy-digestion-healthy-skin/\"><img width=\"1300\" height=\"1300\" src=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/everyday-detox-tea.jpg\" class=\"attachment-full size-full wp-post-image\" alt=\"My Everyday Detox Tea: Because Healthy Digestion = Healthy Skin\" srcset=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/everyday-detox-tea.jpg 1300w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/everyday-detox-tea-150x150.jpg 150w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/everyday-detox-tea-300x300.jpg 300w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/everyday-detox-tea-768x768.jpg 768w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/everyday-detox-tea-1024x1024.jpg 1024w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/everyday-detox-tea-180x180.jpg 180w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/everyday-detox-tea-600x600.jpg 600w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/everyday-detox-tea-250x250.jpg 250w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/everyday-detox-tea-80x80.jpg 80w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/everyday-detox-tea-330x330.jpg 330w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/everyday-detox-tea-160x160.jpg 160w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/everyday-detox-tea-293x293.jpg 293w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1300px) 100vw, 1300px\"></a></div>\n<div class=\"entry-content\" itemprop=\"articleBody\">\n<p>An easy and EFFECTIVE&nbsp;everyday detox tea? <em>Yes please. </em></p>\n<p>I’m a tea junkie. I can’t say enough about the importance of tea and the calm it gives me. Whether it’s hot or cold, tea is basically a liquid hug that aids in digestion, eliminates toxins, clears the skin and is one of the best kept skinny secrets out there (besides <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/the-easiest-cheapest-best-beauty-tip/\" target=\"_blank\">this</a>).</p>\n<p>I down about 3-5 cups a day. I’ve been drinking tea since I was 6 years old (my Mom is Persian and tea is a big part of the culture/cuisine, so she would always make me fresh herbal tea as a kid).</p>\n<p>I don’t drink caffeine. It gives me horrible <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/how-to-overcome-social-anxiety-self-sabotage/\" target=\"_blank\">anxiety</a> for whatever reason, so that cuts out a lot of options. I also don’t drink teas that are dark unless I have one of <a href=\"http://rstyle.me/n/cizzkmb7xs7\" target=\"_blank\">these</a> straws (I know I’m weird but trust me, it prevents stains, preserves your tooth enamel and helps keep your <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/giveaway-smile-brilliant-for-the-new-year/\" target=\"_blank\">smile white</a>).</p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">I’m all about NATURALLY&nbsp;detoxifying, de-bloating, flushing, regulating, digesting and keeping things “moving along,” on a daily basis (both physically AND emotionally. Ha!),&nbsp;through <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/my-diet-the-everyday-smoothie/\" target=\"_blank\">my diet</a>&nbsp;and <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/my-1-secret-to-staying-fit/\" target=\"_blank\">staying fit</a>.</h4>\n<p>Every morning, I start off with <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/because-clear-skin-better-moods-and-looking-good-naked-is-always-a-plus/\" target=\"_blank\">hot lemon water</a>&nbsp;and throughout the day, I drink fresh mint&nbsp;tea and lots of <a href=\"http://rstyle.me/n/ciz3evb7xs7\" target=\"_blank\">water</a>.</p>\n<p>Although I’m very selective with dried teas, I do&nbsp;drink tea with dried teabags on occasion, but really – there’s just no comparison&nbsp;to fresh tea.</p>\n<p>When it comes to flavor and quality, you always want to go fresh whenever possible. <em>Why?</em>&nbsp;Some dried tea leaves can be overly&nbsp;acidic (which could&nbsp;disrupt&nbsp;your&nbsp;pH), dehydrating (no thanks), and can taste very bitter (so you end up adding sugar that you don’t need; sugar that causes inflammation, <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/my-diet-the-everyday-smoothie/\" target=\"_blank\">candida</a>&nbsp;overgrowth&nbsp;and dis-ease within your body).</p>\n<p>With freshly brewed tea, there’s a natural sweetness – no bitter taste.</p>\n<p>When you use fresh mint leaves to brew tea, it&nbsp;allows the essential oil from the leaves to release into the water (&amp; you get so many more added benefits).</p>\n<h3 style=\"text-align: center;\">Here’s the everyday detox tea that I drink…</h3>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><em>Get ready to say bye to indigestion, reflux, bloat and inflammation of the gut.&nbsp;</em></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"> <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/my-everyday-detox-tea-healthy-digestion-healthy-skin/#more-28421\" class=\"more-link button outline small\">Continue Reading</a></p>\n</div>\n<div When To Fold\" srcset=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/emotional-investment.jpg 1146w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/emotional-investment-264x300.jpg 264w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/emotional-investment-768x871.jpg 768w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/emotional-investment-903x1024.jpg 903w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1146px) 100vw, 1146px\"></a></div>\n<div class=\"entry-content\" itemprop=\"articleBody\">\n<p>Emotional investment seems like the most no-brainer, autopilot investment because it comes from the heart. If we aren’t self aware, we buy into the bullsh*t that “what our&nbsp;heart wants,” is in no way convoluted by our negative belief system, <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/daddy-issues-15-signs-you-may-have-them/\" target=\"_blank\">childhood</a>, un-dealt-with trauma, <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/social-media-and-relationships-5-red-flags/\" target=\"_blank\">insecurities</a>, triggers and <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/how-to-be-fearless-confident-start-living-your-dreams/\" target=\"_blank\">fears</a>.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">So&nbsp;what do we do? Approve the investment and go with our heart.</p>\n<h4>Unlike financial investments which have disclosures, the “disclosure” of emotional investment is never really disclosed until the cost has already been incurred.</h4>\n<p>A few years ago, Bernie Madoff was all over the news. Madoff was the self-admitted operator of a Ponzi scheme that is considered to this day, to be the single largest financial fraud in United States history. Madoff’s&nbsp;unknowing investors&nbsp;were some of the most well-known, accomplished, talented and intelligent people.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">So why did some&nbsp;<em>continue&nbsp;</em>to invest <em>despite</em><i>&nbsp;</i>dwindling&nbsp;returns?</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">Why did many invest&nbsp;<em>even when&nbsp;</em>there were whisperings of corruption?</p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">Talent, intelligence, notoriety and accomplishment do not make you immune to emotional investment without returns.</h4>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\">I’m not going to speak for anyone because I don’t want to, it’s not my place&nbsp;to and I’m not educated enough on the matter. So many lives were destroyed and are destroyed everyday in Ponzi schemes – financial<em> and </em>emotional.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">What I can&nbsp;do, is offer my opinion on why investment continues, despite&nbsp;conditions which make a return impossible.</p>\n<h4>When the environment surrounding the investor&nbsp;is&nbsp;no longer conducive to the security and solidity that she/he was initially promised and assured, any continued investments thereafter HAVE TO&nbsp;be&nbsp;emotionally based.</h4>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><em>Why? </em></p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: left;\">Because reality-based logic can&nbsp;no longer stand a chance; security now needs to be concocted. The mechanism itself is&nbsp;now the illogical nucleus of something that’s too painful and unbelievable to face.</h4>\n<p>I feel like at this point, many of us will&nbsp;continue to invest (despite not seeing promised returns), because by continuing to invest, it shows that we&nbsp;still believe in the investment (and aren’t&nbsp;going&nbsp;to invest our&nbsp;attention in any of&nbsp;the “hearsay” or “haters”).</p>\n<h4>You see everything capsizing around you in slow motion. So, instead of folding, you go for a strong right hook in the name of emotional investment.</h4>\n<h4>You think to yourself: “If I show through my actions that no matter what, I won’t give up&nbsp;and I AM going to continue to invest (no matter how sh*t the return)…&nbsp;I&nbsp;<em>have&nbsp;</em>to, at SOME POINT, be noticed, appreciated and see a return…&nbsp;<em>Right?”</em></h4>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">I’ve&nbsp;experienced this time and time again in my life – never knowing when to fold and only folding when circumstances, relationsh*ts, LIFE, etc., folded for me.</p>\n<h3 style=\"text-align: center;\">Here’s my experience with emotional investment – how to know&nbsp;when to hold’em &amp; how to Jedi master the art of folding:</h3>\n<p> <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/making-emotional-investment-invest-fold/#more-28400\" class=\"more-link button outline small\">Continue Reading</a></p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"df-affiliate\"><h4 has-post-thumbnail hentry category-breakups category-exes category-heartbreak category-relationships tag-heartbreak tag-loss df-standard\" itemscope=\"\" itemtype=\"http://schema.org/NewsArticle\" itemprop=\"blogPost\" role=\"article\">\n<div class=\"df-post-title  aligncenter\" onclick=\"void(0)\"><div class=\"boxed-wrap\"><div class=\"df-single-category\"><span class=\"entry-terms category\" itemprop=\"articleSection\"><a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/category/relationships/breakups/\" rel=\"category tag\">BREAKUPS</a>, <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/category/relationships/exes/\" rel=\"category tag\">EXES</a>, <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/category/relationships/heartbreak/\" rel=\"category tag\">HEARTBREAK</a>, <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/category/relationships/\" rel=\"category tag\">RELATIONSHIPS</a></span></div><h2 class=\"entry-title  display-3\" itemprop=\"headline\"><a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/how-to-stop-missing-someone-when-youre-heartbroken/\" title=\"HOW TO STOP MISSING SOMEONE WHEN YOU’RE HEARTBROKEN\">HOW TO STOP MISSING SOMEONE WHEN YOU’RE HEARTBROKEN</a></h2><div class=\"df-post-on\"><time class=\"entry-published updated\" datetime=\"2017-03-12T08:55:51+00:00\" title=\"Sunday, March 12, 2017, 8:55 am\"><a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/2017/03/12/\"><meta itemprop=\"datePublished\" content=\"March 12, 2017\">March 12, 2017</a></time></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"featured-media  filter_bw\"><a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/how-to-stop-missing-someone-when-youre-heartbroken/\"><img width=\"1191\" height=\"1300\" src=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/natasha-adamo-PMS-how-to-stop-missing-someone-when-youre-heartbroken.jpg\" class=\"attachment-full size-full wp-post-image\" alt=\"Natasha Adamo answers: How To Stop Missing Someone When You're Heartbroken\" srcset=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/natasha-adamo-PMS-how-to-stop-missing-someone-when-youre-heartbroken.jpg 1191w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/natasha-adamo-PMS-how-to-stop-missing-someone-when-youre-heartbroken-275x300.jpg 275w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/natasha-adamo-PMS-how-to-stop-missing-someone-when-youre-heartbroken-768x838.jpg 768w, https://postmalesyndrome.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/natasha-adamo-PMS-how-to-stop-missing-someone-when-youre-heartbroken-938x1024.jpg 938w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1191px) 100vw, 1191px\"></a></div>\n<div class=\"entry-content\" itemprop=\"articleBody\">\n<p>How to stop missing someone is one of those subjects&nbsp;that I’ve tried to avoid&nbsp;writing about, just because of the sheer impossibility of it.&nbsp;ALL I want to do is help people out of pain, suffering, self sabotage and patterns that I know all too well. So,&nbsp;<em>how</em> could I&nbsp;reduce to a light switch,&nbsp;the kind of pain and longing that hijacks your joy, your consciousness, your thoughts and your heart?</p>\n<p>How could I remedy through my words, a wound that runs so deep, it allows your&nbsp;<a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/how-to-be-fearless-confident-start-living-your-dreams/\" target=\"_blank\">deepest fears</a> to burst&nbsp;out of a closet that you thought you had bolted shut?</p>\n<p>I didn’t think I&nbsp;could I compete with that kind of wildfire, until I found myself in the middle of a blaze&nbsp;bigger than&nbsp;ever before.</p>\n<p>I get asked everyday, “How do I stop missing him/her? I’ll do anything. I just want to stop feeling this pain. I’m exhausted… <em>but I just can’t.let.go.&nbsp;</em>HELP.”</p>\n<p>And I’ve been there. OMG have I been there.</p>\n<p>I get it, I feel your pain and I’m feeling it with you right now. Although my current pain&nbsp;isn’t rooted in romance, it doesn’t matter.&nbsp;<em>Pa</em><em>in is pain.&nbsp;</em>This isn’t a competition, this is something that we ALL feel and every ounce of it is valid because it’s OURS.</p>\n<p>Since my Grandma died a few weeks ago, I wake up every morning feeling like I’m drowning. I have good moments, but the pain of missing her seems to have a radar that extinguishes any kind of inch toward movement. Experiencing the death of a loved one&nbsp;is excruciating, but at the very least, comfort can be found in the finality that death embodies. Finality is an extremely painful and difficult reality to accept, but you can rely on the knowingness&nbsp;that it’ll never change and thus, organically and at your own pace, accept, appreciate, grow and evolve.</p>\n<h4>I truly believe that breakups can be&nbsp;harder to deal with than death&nbsp;because with breakups, there’s never really a finality. Death by breakup is always subject to resurrection. It’s weird. You could be completely moved on, a year&nbsp;down the line enjoying yourself at dinner and all of a sudden, you get a “happy birthday!” text.</h4>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">And just like that… they’ve resurrected from the graveyard. If only&nbsp;for a moment.</h4>\n<h4>When it comes to figuring out how to stop missing someone, what do you do when you’re mourning the death of someone that’s living and breathing?</h4>\n<p>I miss my Mom everyday. I miss the person that she was before cancer. Most people wouldn’t notice much because she doesn’t skip a beat, but I do. I miss her and I struggle with how to turn off, or at least lessen that yearning for what was and for what my heart hopes will someday be again. I can never fully trust that hope though, because there’s always this looming fear of the cancer showing up somewhere else, just as it did after her first surgery last year. I beat myself up and&nbsp;feel guilty for even <em>expressing</em>&nbsp;these feelings when her situation could be so much&nbsp;worse.</p>\n<h4>That’s the thing with pain though. Not only does it NOT discriminate, but once it permeates… guilt, self sabotage, fear, anger &amp; a destructive level of MISSING, will take on a life of its own as long as you continue&nbsp;fertilizing&nbsp;it.</h4>\n<p>This got me thinking about past relationships and <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/how-to-let-him-go-get-over-the-pain-of-losing-your-ex/\" target=\"_blank\">missing exes</a>. I remember missing an ex so much, everyone that I encountered did nothing but highlight every detail of his absence.&nbsp;My decisions, lack of maturity and lack of honesty&nbsp;were a big reason for the relationship ending. Because of that, I began to disproportionately beat myself up after he dumped me, sinking lower and lower into “I’ll-never-get-over-him-or-love-again,” hell.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><em>&amp; that’s when the sh*t really hit the fan.</em></p>\n<h4>As I sunk lower and lower into the self blame, I didn’t realize that because I had sunk so low, I would have&nbsp;to look up higher and higher whenever I thought of him. This inverted pedestaling, not only upped my feelings of <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/how-to-turn-your-life-around/\" target=\"_blank\">hopelessness</a>, but it caused complete blindness to <em>his&nbsp;</em>shortcomings.</h4>\n<h4>Because I was so&nbsp;busy beating myself up and doing everything&nbsp;I could to re-traumatize and reaffirm that I was indeed forgettable, discardable and worthless, I failed to&nbsp;remember that there were 2 PEOPLE in the relationship with their OWN&nbsp;shortcomings and faults.</h4>\n<p>There was nothing I could do except watch (through a fake <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/social-media-and-relationships-5-red-flags/\" target=\"_blank\">social media</a> account because I had been blocked), how his life was so much better without me in it. How could he not miss me&nbsp;and just be so okay? How could he just forget about me and everything we had?</p>\n<h4>It doesn’t matter if you’re trying to figure out how to stop missing an ex&nbsp;that <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/is-he-emotionally-available/\" target=\"_blank\">wasn’t good for you</a>, an ex&nbsp;that was the <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/am-i-codependent-3-ways-to-heal-codependency-now/\" target=\"_blank\">love of your life</a> or if you’re dealing with death or&nbsp;another kind of loss.</h4>\n<p>WHAT REALLY MATTERS:&nbsp;you need a way out of the pain, out of the stagnation and OUT of the life-robbing MISSING-ness.</p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\">Here’s how to stop missing someone when you’re so heartbroken, you feel like you’ve already died an emotional death.</h4>\n<p> <a href=\"https://postmalesyndrome.com/how-to-stop-missing-someone-when-youre-heartbroken/#more-28357\" class=\"more-link button outline small\">Continue Reading</a></p>\n</div>\n<div
